result.variant not in summary.results_by_variant:\n                summary.results_by_variant[result.variant] = []\n            summary.results_by_variant[result.variant].append(result)\n        \n        # Calculate metrics for each variant\n        for variant, results in summary.results_by_variant.items():\n            if not results:\n                continue\n            \n            # Sample size\n            summary.samples_by_variant[variant] = len(results)\n            \n            # Accuracy\n            correct = sum(1 for r in results if r.was_correct)\n            summary.accuracy_by_variant[variant] = correct / len(results)\n            \n            # Average confidence\n            avg_confidence = sum(r.confidence for r in results) / len(results)\n            summary.avg_confidence_by_variant[variant] = avg_confidence\n            \n            # Average response time\n            avg_time = sum(r.response_time_ms for r in results) / len(results)\n            summary.avg_response_time_by_variant[variant] = avg_time\n        \n        # Check statistical significance\n        summary.is_significant, summary.p_value = self._check_significance(summary)\n        \n        # Determine winner\n        if summary.is_significant:\n            summary.winner = max(\n                summary.accuracy_by_variant.keys(),\n                key=lambda v: summary.accuracy_by_variant[v]\n            )\n        \n        return summary\n    \n    def _check_significance(self, summary: ABTestSummary) -> tuple[bool, float]:\n        """Check if results are statistically significant"""\n        \n        # Simple chi-square test for significance\n        # In production, would use proper statistical tests\n        \n        if len(summary.results_by_variant) < 2:\n            return False, 1.0\n        \n        # Check minimum sample size\n        for variant, count in summary.samples_by_variant.items():\n            if count < self.config.min_samples_per_variant:\n                return False, 1.0\n        \n        # Calculate p-value (simplified)\n        accuracies = list(summary.accuracy_by_variant.values())\n        if len(accuracies) < 2:\n            return False, 1.0\n        \n        # Simple difference test\n        diff = abs(accuracies[0] - accuracies[1])\n        \n        # Rough approximation: larger differences are more significant\n        if diff > 0.05:  # 5% difference\n            p_value = 0.01\n        elif diff > 0.03:  # 3% difference\n            p_value = 0.05\n        else:\n            p_value = 0.5\n        \n        is_significant = p_value < (1.0 - self.config.confidence_level)\n        \n        return is_significant, p_value\n    \n    def should_stop_test(self) -> bool:\n        """Determine if test should be stopped early"""\n        \n        summary = self.get_summary()\n        \n        # Stop if statistically significant and minimum samples reached\n        if summary.is_significant:\n            min_samples = min(summary.samples_by_variant.values())\n            if min_samples >= self.config.min_samples_per_variant:\n                return True\n        \n        # Stop if end date reached\n        if self.config.end_date and datetime.utcnow() > self.config.end_date:\n            return True\n        \n        return False\n    \n    def get_recommendation(self) -> str:\n        """Get recommendation based on test results"""\n        \n        summary = self.get_summary()\n        \n        if not summary.is_significant:\n            return "Continue testing - results not yet statistically significant"\n        \n        if summary.winner:\n            winner_accuracy = summary.accuracy_by_variant[summary.winner]\n            return (\n                f"Deploy {summary.winner.value} - "\n                f"significantly better accuracy ({winner_accuracy:.2%})"\n            )\n        \n        return "Results inconclusive"\n\n\nclass GradualRollout:\n    """Manages gradual rollout of shadow agent"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, initial_traffic: float = 0.1):\n        self.current_traffic = initial_traffic\n        self.rollout_history: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n    \n    def should_use_shadow_agent(self) -> bool:\n        """Determine if shadow agent should be used for this request"""\n        return random.random() < self.current_traffic\n    \n    def increase_traffic(self, increment: float = 0.1):\n        """Increase traffic to shadow agent"""\n        \n        old_traffic = self.current_traffic\n        self.current_traffic = min(1.0, self.current_traffic + increment)\n        \n        self.rollout_history.append({\n            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            "old_traffic": old_traffic,\n            "new_traffic": self.current_traffic,\n            "action": "increase"\n        })\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Increased shadow agent traffic: {old_traffic:.1%} -> {self.current_traffic:.1%}"\n        )\n    \n    def decrease_traffic(self, decrement: float = 0.1):\n        """Decrease traffic to shadow agent"""\n        \n        old_traffic = self.current_traffic\n        self.current_traffic = max(0.0, self.current_traffic - decrement)\n        \n        self.rollout_history.append({\n            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            "old_traffic": old_traffic,\n            "new_traffic": self.current_traffic,\n            "action": "decrease"\n        })\n        \n        logger.info(\n            f"Decreased shadow agent traffic: {old_traffic:.1%} -> {self.current_traffic:.1%}"\n        )\n    \n    def auto_adjust(self, performance_metrics: Dict[str, float]):\n        """Automatically adjust traffic based on performance"""\n        \n        accuracy = performance_metrics.get("accuracy", 0.0)\n        error_rate = performance_metrics.get("error_rate", 0.0)\n        \n        # Increase traffic if performing well\n        if accuracy > 0.9 and error_rate < 0.05:\n            self.increase_traffic(0.1)\n        \n        # Decrease traffic if performing poorly\n        elif accuracy < 0.7 or error_rate > 0.1:\n            self.decrease_traffic(0.1)\n    \n    def get_rollout_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get current rollout status"""\n        \n        return {\n            "current_traffic": self.current_traffic,\n            "rollout_stage": self._get_rollout_stage(),\n            "history_length": len(self.rollout_history),\n            "latest_change": self.rollout_history[-1] if self.rollout_history else None,\n        }\n    \n    def _get_rollout_stage(self) -> str:\n        """Get current rollout stage"""\n        \n        if self.current_traffic == 0.0:\n            return "not_started"\n        elif self.current_traffic < 0.25:\n            return "canary"\n        elif self.current_traffic < 0.5:\n            return "early_rollout"\n        elif self.current_traffic < 0.75:\n            return "mid_rollout"\n        elif self.current_traffic < 1.0:\n            return "late_rollout"\n        else:\n            return "full_deployment"\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

y_true: List, y_pred: List) -> Tuple[float, float, float]:\n        """Calculate precision, recall, F1"""\n        \n        # Binary classification\n        tp = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true == 1 and pred == 1)\n        fp = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true == 0 and pred == 1)\n        fn = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true == 1 and pred == 0)\n        \n        precision = tp / (tp + fp) if (tp + fp) > 0 else 0.0\n        recall = tp / (tp + fn) if (tp + fn) > 0 else 0.0\n        f1 = 2 * (precision * recall) / (precision + recall) if (precision + recall) > 0 else 0.0\n        \n        return precision, recall, f1\n    \n    def _calculate_confusion_matrix(self, y_true: List, y_pred: List) -> List[List[int]]:\n        """Calculate confusion matrix"""\n        \n        # Get unique classes\n        classes = sorted(set(y_true + y_pred))\n        n_classes = len(classes)\n        \n        # Initialize matrix\n        matrix = [[0] * n_classes for _ in range(n_classes)]\n        \n        # Fill matrix\n        class_to_idx = {c: i for i, c in enumerate(classes)}\n        for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred):\n            true_idx = class_to_idx[true]\n            pred_idx = class_to_idx[pred]\n            matrix[true_idx][pred_idx] += 1\n        \n        return matrix\n    \n    def _calculate_per_class_metrics(\n        self,\n        y_true: List,\n        y_pred: List\n    ) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]:\n        """Calculate per-class metrics"""\n        \n        classes = cls and pred == cls)\n            fp = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true != cls and pred == cls)\n            fn = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true == cls and pred != cls)\n            tn = sum(1 for true, pred in zip(y_true, y_pred) if true != cls and pred != cls)\n            \n            precision = tp / (tp + fp) if (tp + fp) > 0 else 0.0\n     n_bins = 10\n        bin_boundaries = [i / n_bins for i in range(n_bins + 1)]\n        \n        ece = 0.0\n        \n        for i in range(n_bins):\n            # Get predictions in this bin\n            lower = bin_boundaries[i]\n            upper = bin_boundaries[i + 1]\n            \n            bin_indices = [\n                j for j, proba in enumerate(y_proba)\n                if lower <= max(proba) < upper\n            ]\n            \n            if not bin_indices:\n                continue\n            \n            # Calculate accuracy and confidence in bin\n            bin_accuracy = sum(\n                1 for j in bin_indices\n                if y_true[j] == (1 if y_proba[j][1] > 0.5 else 0)\n            ) / len(bin_indices)\n            \n            bin_confidence = sum(max(y_proba[j]) for j in bin_indices) / len(bin_indices)\n            \n            # Add to ECE\n            ece += abs(bin_accuracy - bin_confidence) * len(bin_indices) / len(y_true)\n        \n        return ece\n\n\nclass AutomatedTestSuite:\n    """Automated testing suite for shadow agent"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.test_results: List[Dict[str,    def get_trend_analysis(self, metric_name: str, hours: int = 24) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Analyze trend for a specific metric"""\n        \n        cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - return {}\n        \n        # Get metric values\n        values = []\n        for m in recent_metrics:\n            if hasattr(m, metric_name):\n                values.append(getattr(m, \n        trend = "improving" if avg_second > avg_first else "declining" if avg_second < avg_first else "stable"\n        change_pct = ((avg_second - avg_first) / avg_first * 100) if avg_first > 0         if alert.id == alert_id:\n                alert.is_resolved = True\n                alert.resolved_at = datetime.utcnow()\n                self.active_alerts.remove(alert)\n                logger.info(f"Alert resolved: {alert.title}")\n                break\n    \n    def _send_notifications(self, alert: Alert):\n        """Send alert notifications"""\n        \n        # In production, would send to configured channels\n        # (email, Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)\n        logger.info(f"Notification sent for alert: {alert.title}")\n    \n    def get_dashboard_data(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get complete dashboard data"""\n        \n        current_metrics = self.get_current_metrics()\n        summary_24h = self.get_metrics_summary(hours=24)\n        \n        return {\n            "current_metrics": current_metrics.__dict__ if current_metrics else {},\n            "summary_24h": summary_24h,\n            "active_alerts": [\n                {\n                    "id": str(a.id),\n                    "severity": a.severity,\n                    "title": a.title,\n                    "message": a.message,\n                    "created_at": a.created_at.isoformat(),\n                }\n                for a in self.active_alerts\n            ],\n            "trends": {\n                "accuracy": self.get_trend_analysis("accuracy", hours=24),\n                "response_time": self.get_trend_analysis("avg_response_time_ms", hours=24),\n                "error_rate": self.get_trend_analysis("error_rate", hours=24),\n            },\n        }\n\n\nclass FeedbackLoop:\n    """Implements continuous feedback loop for model improvement"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.feedback_queue: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n        self.improvement_history: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []\n    \n    def collect_feedback(\n        self,\n        prediction_id: UUID,\n        actual_outcome: Any,\n        was_correct: bool,\n        user_feedback: Optional[str] = None\n    ):\n        """Collect feedback on a prediction"""\n        \n        feedback = {\n            "prediction_id": str(prediction_id),\n            "actual_outcome": actual_outcome,\n            "was_correct": was_correct,\n            "user_feedback": user_feedback,\n            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n        }\n        \n        self.feedback_queue.append(feedback)\n        \n        logger.info(f"Feedback collected: correct={was_correct}")\n    \n    def process_feedback_batch(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Process batch of feedback for model improvement"""\n        \n        if not self.feedback_queue:\n            return {"processed": 0}\n        \n        # Analyze feedback\n        total = len(self.feedback_queue)\n        correct = sum(1 for f in self.feedback_queue if f["was_correct"])\n        accuracy = correct / total if total > 0 else 0\n        \n        # Identify improvement opportunities\n        incorrect_predictions = [\n            f for f in self.feedback_queue if not f["was_correct"]\n        ]\n        \n        improvement_summary = {\n            "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n            "total_feedback": total,\n            "accuracy": accuracy,\n            "incorrect_predictions": len(incorrect_predictions),\n            "improvement_opportunities": self._identify_improvements(incorrect_predictions),\n        }\n        \n        self.improvement_history.append(improvement_summary)\n        \n        # Clear queue\n        self.feedback_queue = []\n        \n        logger.info(f"Processed {total} feedback items, accuracy: {accuracy:.2%}")\n        \n        return improvement_summary\n    \n    def _identify_improvements(self, incorrect_predictions: List[Dict]) -> List[str]:\n        """Identify improvement opportunities from incorrect predictions"""\n        \n        opportunities = []\n        \n        if len(incorrect_predictions) > 10:\n            opportunities.append("High error rate - consider retraining model")\n        \n        # Analyze patterns in errors\n        # In production, would do more sophisticated analysis\n        \n        return opportunities\n    \n    def get_improvement_recommendations(self) -> List[str]:\n        """Get recommendations for model improvement"""\n        \n        if not self.improvement_history:\n            return ["Collect more feedback data"]\n        \n        recent = self.improvement_history[-1]\n        recommendations = []\n        \n        if recent["accuracy"] < 0.8:\n            recommendations.append("Model accuracy below 80% - retrain with recent corrections")\n        \n        if recent["incorrect_predictions"] > 50:\n            recommendations.append("High number of errors - review feature engineering")\n        \n        recommendations.extend(recent.get("improvement_opportunities", []))\n        \n        return recommendations\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Model training\n        self.training_pipeline = TrainingPipeline(\n            TrainingConfig(checkpoint_dir=checkpoint_dir)\n        )\n        self.hyperparameter_tuner = HyperparameterTuner()\n        \n        # Evaluation and monitoring\n        self.evaluator = ModelEvaluator()\n        self.test_suite = AutomatedTestSuite()\n        self.monitoring = MonitoringDashboard()\n        self.feedback_loop = FeedbackLoop()\n        \n        # A/B testing and rollout\n        self.ab_test: Optional[ABTestFramework] = None\n        self.gradual_rollout = GradualRollout(initial_traffic=0.1)\n        \n        logger.info("Shadow Agent System initialized")\n    \n    def train_from_corrections(\n        self,\n        corrections: List[Correction],\n        model_name: str = "shadow_agent",\n        model_version: str = "1.0.0",\n        tune_hyperparameters: bool = False\n    ) -> UUID:\n        """Train shadow agent from corrections"""\n        \n        logger.info(f"Training shadow agent from {len(corrections)} corrections")\n        \n        # Step 1: Transform corrections to training data\n        logger.info("Step 1: Transforming corrections to training data...")\n        dataset = self.data_transformer.transform_corrections(corrections)\n        \n        # Step 2: Feature engineering\n        logger.info("Step 2: Applying feature engineering...")\n        dataset = self.feature_engineer.fit_transform(dataset)\n        \n        # Step 3: Data validation\n        logger.info("Step 3: Validating data quality...")\n        quality_metrics = self.data_validator.validate_dataset(dataset)\n        logger.info(f"Data quality score: {quality_metrics.overall_quality_score:.2f}")\n        \n        if quality_metrics.overall_quality_score < 0.5:\n            logger.warning("Low data quality - training may not be effective")\n        \n        # Step 4: Split data\n        logger.info("Step 4: Splitting data...")\n        dataset = self.data_splitter.split_dataset(dataset, strategy="stratified")\n        \n        # Step 5: Hyperparameter tuning (optional)\n        model_config = None\n        if tune_hyperparameters:\n            logger.info("Step 5: Tuning hyperparameters...")\n            param_space = get_default_param_space(ModelType.HYBRID)\n            tuning_result = self.hyperparameter_tuner.tune(\n                ModelType.HYBRID,\n                dataset,\n                param_space\n            )\n            logger.info(f"Best parameters: {tuning_result.best_params}")\n            # Would use best_params to create config\n        \n        # Step 6: Train model\n        logger.info("Step 6: Training model...")\n        model = ModelFactory.create_model(ModelType.HYBRID, model_config)\n        trained_model = self.training_pipeline.train(model, dataset)\n        \n        # Step 7: Evaluate model\n        logger.info("Step 7: Evaluating model...")\n        eval_metrics = self.evaluator.evaluate(trained_model, dataset)\n        logger.info(\n            f"Evaluation: accuracy={eval_metrics.accuracy:.4f}, "\n            f"f1={eval_metrics.f1_score:.4f}"\n        )\n        \n        # Step 8: Run automated tests\n        logger.info("Step 8: Running automated tests...")\n        test_results = self.test_suite.run_all_tests(trained_model, dataset)\n        \n        if not test_results["overall_passed"]:\n            logger.warning("Some tests failed - review before deployment")\n        \n        # Step 9: Register model\n        logger.info("Step 9: Registering model...")\n        model_version_obj = self.model_registry.register_model(\n            trained_model,\n            name=model_name,\n            version=model_version,\n            tags=["trained_from_corrections"]\n        )\n        \n        logger.info(f"Training complete: model_id={model_version_obj.id}")\n        \n        return model_version_obj.id\n    \n    def deploy_model(\n        self,\n        model_id: UUID,\n        environment: str = "production",\n        use_ab_test: bool = False,\n        use_gradual_rollout: bool = True\n    ):\n        """Deploy model to production"""\n        \n        logger.info(f"Deploying model {model_id} to {environment}")\n        \n        # Deploy to registry\n        model_version = self.model_registry.deploy_model(model_id, environment)\n        \n        # Update shadow agent\n        self.shadow_agent.update_model(model_version)\n        \n        # Setup A/B test if requested\n        if use_ab_test:\n            logger.info("Setting up A/B test...")\n            ab_config = ABTestConfig(\n                name=f"shadow_agent_vs_murphy_gate_{model_version.version}",\n                variants={\n                    VariantType.SHADOW_AGENT: 0.5,\n                    VariantType.MURPHY_GATE: 0.5,\n                },\n                primary_metric="accuracy",\n            )\n            self.ab_test = ABTestFramework(ab_config)\n        \n        # Setup gradual rollout if requested\n        if use_gradual_rollout:\n            logger.info("Starting gradual rollout...")\n            self.gradual_rollout = GradualRollout(initial_traffic=0.1)\n        \n        logger.info("Deployment complete")\n    \n    def make_prediction(\n        self,\n        input_features: Dict[str, Any],\n        task_id: Optional[UUID] = None,\n        use_fallback: bool = True\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Make prediction using shadow agent"""\n        \n        # Check if should use shadow agent (gradual rollout)\n        if not self.gradual_rollout.should_use_shadow_agent():\n            return {\n                "source": "murphy_gate",\n                "prediction": None,\n                "confidence": 0.0,\n                "reason": "gradual_rollout"\n            }\n        \n        # Make prediction\n        prediction = self.shadow_agent.predict(\n            input_features=input_features,\n            task_id=task_id\n        )\n        \n        # Check if confidence is sufficient\n        if use_fallback and prediction.confidence < self.shadow_agent.config.fallback_threshold:\n            return {\n                "source": "murphy_gate_fallback",\n                "prediction": prediction.prediction,\n                "confidence": prediction.confidence,\n                "reason": "low_confidence"\n            }\n        \n        return {\n            "source": "shadow_agent",\n            "prediction": prediction.prediction,\n            "confidence": prediction.confidence,\n            "prediction_id": str(prediction.id)\n        }\n    \n    def record_feedback(\n        self,\n        prediction_id: UUID,\n        actual_outcome: Any,\n        was_correct: bool,\n        user_feedback: Optional[str] = None\n    ):\n        """Record feedback on a prediction"""\n        \n        self.feedback_loop.collect_feedback(\n            prediction_id=prediction_id,\n            actual_outcome=actual_outcome,\n            was_correct=was_correct,\n            user_feedback=user_feedback\n        )\n    \n    def process_feedback_and_improve(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Process feedback and get improvement recommendations"""\n        \n        # Process feedback batch\n        summary = self.feedback_loop.process_feedback_batch()\n        \n        # Get recommendations\n        recommendations = self.feedback_loop.get_improvement_recommendations()\n        \n        # Auto-adjust rollout based on performance\n        if summary.get("accuracy", 0) > 0.9:\n            self.gradual_rollout.increase_traffic(0.1)\n        elif summary.get("accuracy", 0) < 0.7:\n            self.gradual_rollout.decrease_traffic(0.1)\n        \n        return {\n            "summary": summary,\n            "recommendations": recommendations,\n            "rollout_status": self.gradual_rollout.get_rollout_status(),\n        }\n    \n    def get_system_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get complete system status"""\n        \n        return {\n            "shadow_agent": {\n                "model_loaded": self.shadow_agent.current_model is not None,\n                "prediction_stats": self.shadow_agent.get_prediction_stats(),\n            },\n            "model_registry": self.model_registry.get_registry_summary(),\n            "monitoring": self.monitoring.get_dashboard_data(),\n            "rollout": self.gradual_rollout.get_rollout_status(),\n            "ab_test": self.ab_test.get_summary().__dict__ if self.ab_test else None,\n        }\n\n\n# Convenience function for quick setup\ndef create_shadow_agent_system(\n    model_registry_dir: str = "model_registry",\n    checkpoint_dir: str = "checkpoints"\n) -> ShadowAgentSystem:\n    """Create and initialize shadow agent system"""\n    \n    return ShadowAgentSystem(\n        model_registry_dir=model_registry_dir,\n        checkpoint_dir=checkpoint_dir\n    )\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/deployment/scripts/deploy.sh">\n#!/bin/bash\n\n# Murphy System Deployment Script\n# Usage: ./deploy.sh [environment] [version]\n\nset -e\n\nENVIRONMENT=${1:-production}\nVERSION=${2:-latest}\nNAMESPACE="murphy-system"\n\necho "=========================================="\necho "Murphy System Deployment"\necho "=========================================="\necho "Environment: $ENVIRONMENT"\necho "Version: $VERSION"\necho "Namespace: $NAMESPACE"\necho "=========================================="\n\n# Color codes\nRED=\'\\033[0;31m\'\nGREEN=\'\\033[0;32m\'\nYELLOW=\'\\033[1;33m\'\nNC=\'\\033[0m\' # No Color\n\n# Functions\nlog_info() {\n    echo -e "${GREEN}[INFO]${NC} $1"\n}\n\nlog_warn() {\n    echo -e "${YELLOW}[WARN]${NC} $1"\n}\n\nlog_error() {\n    echo -e "${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1"\n}\n\n# Check prerequisites\ncheck_prerequisites() {\n    log_info "Checking prerequisites..."\n    \n    if ! command -v kubectl &> /dev/null; then\n        log_error "kubectl not found. Please install kubectl."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    if ! command -v docker &> /dev/null; then\n        log_error "docker not found. Please install docker."\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    log_info "Prerequisites check passed"\n}\n\n# Build Docker image\nbuild_image() {\n    log_info "Building Docker image..."\n    \n    cd ../..\n    docker build -t murphy-system:$VERSION -f murphy_implementation/deployment/Dockerfile .\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Docker image built successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Docker image build failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Push Docker image\npush_image() {\n    log_info "Pushing Docker image to registry..."\n    \n    # Tag for registry\n    docker tag murphy-system:$VERSION your-registry.com/murphy-system:$VERSION\n    \n    # Push to registry\n    docker push your-registry.com/murphy-system:$VERSION\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Docker image pushed successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Docker image push failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Create namespace\ncreate_namespace() {\n    log_info "Creating namespace..."\n    \n    kubectl apply -f kubernetes/namespace.yaml\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Namespace created/updated successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Namespace creation failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Deploy to Kubernetes\ndeploy_kubernetes() {\n    log_info "Deploying to Kubernetes..."\n    \n    # Apply deployment\n    kubectl apply -f kubernetes/deployment.yaml -n $NAMESPACE\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Deployment applied successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Deployment failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n    \n    # Wait for rollout\n    log_info "Waiting for rollout to complete..."\n    kubectl rollout status deployment/murphy-api -n $NAMESPACE --timeout=5m\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Rollout completed successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Rollout failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Run health checks\nhealth_check() {\n    log_info "Running health checks..."\n    \n    # Get service endpoint\n    SERVICE_IP=$(kubectl get svc murphy-api-service -n $NAMESPACE -o jsonpath=\'{.status.loadBalancer.ingress[0].ip}\')\n    \n    if [ -z "$SERVICE_IP" ]; then\n        log_warn "Service IP not available yet. Skipping health check."\n        return\n    fi\n    \n    # Check health endpoint\n    HEALTH_STATUS=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" http://$SERVICE_IP/health)\n    \n    if [ "$HEALTH_STATUS" == "200" ]; then\n        log_info "Health check passed"\n    else\n        log_error "Health check failed (HTTP $HEALTH_STATUS)"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Rollback deployment\nrollback() {\n    log_warn "Rolling back deployment..."\n    \n    kubectl rollout undo deployment/murphy-api -n $NAMESPACE\n    \n    if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then\n        log_info "Rollback completed successfully"\n    else\n        log_error "Rollback failed"\n        exit 1\n    fi\n}\n\n# Main deployment flow\nmain() {\n    check_prerequisites\n    \n    # Build and push image\n    build_image\n    \n    if [ "$ENVIRONMENT" == "production" ]; then\n        push_image\n    fi\n    \n    # Deploy to Kubernetes\n    create_namespace\n    deploy_kubernetes\n    \n    # Run health checks\n    sleep 10\n    health_check\n    \n    log_info "=========================================="\n    log_info "Deployment completed successfully!"\n    log_info "=========================================="\n    \n    # Show deployment info\n    kubectl get pods -n $NAMESPACE\n    kubectl get svc -n $NAMESPACE\n}\n\n# Handle errors\ntrap \'log_error "Deployment failed. Run ./deploy.sh rollback to revert."; exit 1\' ERR\n\n# Run deployment\nif [ "$1" == "rollback" ]; then\n    rollback\nelse\n    main\nfi\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/deployment/RUNBOOK.md">\n# Murphy System Operations Runbook\n\n## Table of Contents\n1. [Common Issues](#common-issues)\n2. [Emergency Procedures](#emergency-procedures)\n3. [Monitoring and Alerts](#monitoring-and-alerts)\n4. [Deployment Procedures](#deployment-procedures)\n5. [Troubleshooting Guide](#troubleshooting-guide)\n\n---\n\n## Common Issues\n\n### Issue 1: High Error Rate\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Error rate > 10%\n- Alert: `HighErrorRate` firing\n- Users reporting failures\n\n**Diagnosis:**\n```bash\n# Check error logs\nkubectl logs -n murphy-system -l app=murphy-api --tail=100 | grep ERROR\n\n# Check error metrics\ncurl http://prometheus:9090/api/v1/query?query=rate(murphy_api_errors_total[5m])\n```\n\n**Resolution:**\n1. Identify error type from logs\n2. Check if it\'s a known issue\n3. If database-related, check database connectivity\n4. If model-related, check shadow agent status\n5. Consider rolling back if errors persist\n\n**Rollback Command:**\n```bash\n./deployment/scripts/deploy.sh rollback\n```\n\n---\n\n### Issue 2: Low Model Accuracy\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Model accuracy < 70%\n- Alert: `LowModelAccuracy` firing\n- High fallback rate to Murphy Gate\n\n**Diagnosis:**\n```bash\n# Check model metrics\ncurl http://murphy-api:8000/api/shadow-agent/stats\n\n# Check recent predictions\nkubectl exec -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx -- python -c "\nfrom murphy_implementation.shadow_agent import create_shadow_agent_system\nsystem = create_shadow_agent_system()\nprint(system.shadow_agent.get_prediction_stats())\n"\n```\n\n**Resolution:**\n1. Check if model is loaded correctly\n2. Review recent training data quality\n3. Check for data drift\n4. Consider retraining model with recent corrections\n5. Temporarily increase fallback threshold\n\n**Retrain Command:**\n```python\nfrom murphy_implementation.shadow_agent import create_shadow_agent_system\n\nsystem = create_shadow_agent_system()\nmodel_id = system.train_from_corrections(\n    corrections=recent_corrections,\n    tune_hyperparameters=True\n)\nsystem.deploy_model(model_id, use_gradual_rollout=True)\n```\n\n---\n\n### Issue 3: High Response Time\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- p95 response time > 1s\n- Alert: `HighResponseTime` firing\n- Slow user experience\n\n**Diagnosis:**\n```bash\n# Check response time distribution\ncurl http://prometheus:9090/api/v1/query?query=histogram_quantile(0.95,rate(murphy_api_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m]))\n\n# Check resource usage\nkubectl top pods -n murphy-system\n```\n\n**Resolution:**\n1. Check if CPU/memory limits are reached\n2. Scale up if needed: `kubectl scale deployment murphy-api -n murphy-system --replicas=5`\n3. Check database query performance\n4. Review slow endpoints in logs\n5. Consider caching frequently accessed data\n\n---\n\n### Issue 4: Service Down\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Alert: `ServiceDown` firing\n- API not responding\n- Health check failing\n\n**Diagnosis:**\n```bash\n# Check pod status\nkubectl get pods -n murphy-system\n\n# Check pod logs\nkubectl logs -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx --tail=50\n\n# Check events\nkubectl get events -n murphy-system --sort-by=\'.lastTimestamp\'\n```\n\n**Resolution:**\n1. Check if pods are running: `kubectl get pods -n murphy-system`\n2. If pods are CrashLooping, check logs for errors\n3. If pods are Pending, check resource availability\n4. Restart deployment if needed: `kubectl rollout restart deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system`\n5. If issue persists, rollback to previous version\n\n---\n\n## Emergency Procedures\n\n### Emergency Rollback\n\n**When to use:**\n- Critical production issue\n- High error rate (>50%)\n- Service completely down\n- Data corruption detected\n\n**Procedure:**\n```bash\n# 1. Immediate rollback\n./deployment/scripts/deploy.sh rollback\n\n# 2. Verify rollback\nkubectl rollout status deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n\n# 3. Check health\ncurl http://murphy-api-service/health\n\n# 4. Monitor metrics\n# Open Grafana dashboard and verify metrics are normal\n\n# 5. Notify team\n# Send notification to #murphy-alerts channel\n```\n\n---\n\n### Emergency Scale-Up\n\n**When to use:**\n- Sudden traffic spike\n- High CPU/memory usage\n- Slow response times\n\n**Procedure:**\n```bash\n# 1. Scale up replicas\nkubectl scale deployment murphy-api -n murphy-system --replicas=10\n\n# 2. Verify scaling\nkubectl get pods -n murphy-system -w\n\n# 3. Monitor performance\n# Check Grafana dashboard for improvements\n\n# 4. Adjust HPA if needed\nkubectl edit hpa murphy-api-hpa -n murphy-system\n```\n\n---\n\n### Emergency Maintenance Mode\n\n**When to use:**\n- Critical bug fix needed\n- Database maintenance\n- Security patch\n\n**Procedure:**\n```bash\n# 1. Enable maintenance mode\nkubectl set env deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system MAINTENANCE_MODE=true\n\n# 2. Scale down to 1 replica\nkubectl scale deployment murphy-api -n murphy-system --replicas=1\n\n# 3. Perform maintenance\n# ... your maintenance tasks ...\n\n# 4. Disable maintenance mode\nkubectl set env deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system MAINTENANCE_MODE=false\n\n# 5. Scale back up\nkubectl scale deployment murphy-api -n murphy-system --replicas=3\n```\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring and Alerts\n\n### Alert Response Matrix\n\n| Alert | Severity | Response Time | Action |\n|-------|----------|---------------|--------|\n| HighErrorRate | Critical | Immediate | Investigate logs, consider rollback |\n| ServiceDown | Critical | Immediate | Check pods, restart if needed |\n| LowModelAccuracy | Warning | 1 hour | Review model performance, plan retrain |\n| HighResponseTime | Warning | 30 minutes | Check resources, scale if needed |\n| HighMemoryUsage | Warning | 1 hour | Monitor, scale if continues |\n| LowDataQuality | Info | 4 hours | Review training data |\n\n### Dashboard Access\n\n- **Grafana:** http://grafana.murphy-system.com\n- **Prometheus:** http://prometheus.murphy-system.com\n- **Kubernetes Dashboard:** http://k8s-dashboard.murphy-system.com\n\n### Key Metrics to Monitor\n\n1. **API Health:**\n   - Request rate\n   - Error rate\n   - Response time (p50, p95, p99)\n\n2. **Model Performance:**\n   - Accuracy\n   - Confidence distribution\n   - Fallback rate\n\n3. **System Resources:**\n   - CPU usage\n   - Memory usage\n   - Disk usage\n\n4. **Business Metrics:**\n   - Shadow agent usage rate\n   - Training data quality\n   - Correction capture rate\n\n---\n\n## Deployment Procedures\n\n### Standard Deployment\n\n```bash\n# 1. Run tests locally\npytest tests/\n\n# 2. Build and test Docker image\ndocker build -t murphy-system:test -f murphy_implementation/deployment/Dockerfile .\ndocker run murphy-system:test python -m pytest\n\n# 3. Deploy to staging\n./deployment/scripts/deploy.sh staging\n\n# 4. Run smoke tests on staging\ncurl http://staging.murphy-system.com/health\n\n# 5. Deploy to production\n./deployment/scripts/deploy.sh production\n\n# 6. Monitor deployment\nkubectl rollout status deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n\n# 7. Verify health\ncurl http://murphy-api-service/health\n```\n\n### Hotfix Deployment\n\n```bash\n# 1. Create hotfix branch\ngit checkout -b hotfix/critical-fix\n\n# 2. Make fix and test\n# ... make changes ...\npytest tests/\n\n# 3. Fast-track deployment\n./deployment/scripts/deploy.sh production latest\n\n# 4. Monitor closely\n# Watch Grafana dashboard for 30 minutes\n\n# 5. Merge to main\ngit checkout main\ngit merge hotfix/critical-fix\n```\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting Guide\n\n### Database Connection Issues\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Database connection errors in logs\n- Timeouts on database operations\n\n**Steps:**\n```bash\n# 1. Check database pod\nkubectl get pods -n murphy-system | grep postgres\n\n# 2. Check database logs\nkubectl logs -n murphy-system postgres-xxx\n\n# 3. Test connection\nkubectl exec -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx -- python -c "\nimport psycopg2\nconn = psycopg2.connect(\'postgresql://murphy:murphy@postgres:5432/murphy\')\nprint(\'Connection successful\')\n"\n\n# 4. Check connection pool\n# Review connection pool settings in application config\n```\n\n---\n\n### Model Loading Issues\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- "No model loaded" errors\n- Shadow agent not making predictions\n\n**Steps:**\n```bash\n# 1. Check model registry\nkubectl exec -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx -- python -c "\nfrom murphy_implementation.shadow_agent import ModelRegistry\nregistry = ModelRegistry()\nprint(registry.get_registry_summary())\n"\n\n# 2. Check deployed model\n# Verify model is marked as deployed in registry\n\n# 3. Reload model\n# Restart pods to reload model\nkubectl rollout restart deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n```\n\n---\n\n### Memory Leaks\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Gradually increasing memory usage\n- OOMKilled pods\n- Slow performance over time\n\n**Steps:**\n```bash\n# 1. Check memory usage trend\n# Open Grafana and check memory usage over 24h\n\n# 2. Get memory profile\nkubectl exec -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx -- python -m memory_profiler\n\n# 3. Restart pods to free memory\nkubectl rollout restart deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n\n# 4. Investigate code for leaks\n# Review recent changes for potential memory leaks\n```\n\n---\n\n## Contact Information\n\n- **On-Call Engineer:** Check PagerDuty schedule\n- **Team Lead:** [email]\n- **DevOps Team:** #devops-murphy\n- **Slack Alerts:** #murphy-alerts\n- **Incident Channel:** #murphy-incidents\n\n---\n\n## Useful Commands\n\n```bash\n# View logs\nkubectl logs -n murphy-system -l app=murphy-api --tail=100 -f\n\n# Get pod status\nkubectl get pods -n murphy-system\n\n# Describe pod\nkubectl describe pod -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx\n\n# Execute command in pod\nkubectl exec -n murphy-system murphy-api-xxx -- command\n\n# Port forward for local access\nkubectl port-forward -n murphy-system svc/murphy-api-service 8000:80\n\n# View resource usage\nkubectl top pods -n murphy-system\n\n# View events\nkubectl get events -n murphy-system --sort-by=\'.lastTimestamp\'\n\n# Scale deployment\nkubectl scale deployment murphy-api -n murphy-system --replicas=5\n\n# Restart deployment\nkubectl rollout restart deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n\n# Check rollout status\nkubectl rollout status deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n\n# View deployment history\nkubectl rollout history deployment/murphy-api -n murphy-system\n```\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/deployment/API_DOCUMENTATION.md">\n# Murphy System API Documentation\n\n## Overview\nThe Murphy System provides a RESTful API for task execution, correction capture, and shadow agent predictions.\n\n**Base URL:** `https://api.murphy-system.com`\n**Version:** v1\n**Authentication:** API Key (Header: `X-API-Key`)\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n1. [Authentication](#authentication)\n2. [Form Submission](#form-submission)\n3. [Task Execution](#task-execution)\n4. [Correction Capture](#correction-capture)\n5. [Shadow Agent](#shadow-agent)\n6. [Monitoring](#monitoring)\n\n---\n\n## Authentication\n\nAll API requests require authentication using an API key.\n\n### Headers\n```\nX-API-Key: your-api-key-here\nContent-Type: application/json\n```\n\n### Example\n```bash\ncurl -H "X-API-Key: your-api-key" \\\n     -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n     https://api.murphy-system.com/health\n```\n\n---\n\n## Form Submission\n\n### Submit Plan Upload Form\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/plan-upload`\n\n**Description:** Upload a pre-defined task plan for execution.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "plan_file": "base64_encoded_file_content",\n  "plan_format": "json",\n  "metadata": {\n    "source": "user_upload",\n    "version": "1.0"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "submission_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "accepted",\n  "plan_id": "uuid",\n  "tasks_count": 10,\n  "estimated_duration_minutes": 30\n}\n```\n\n**Status Codes:**\n- `200 OK` - Plan accepted\n- `400 Bad Request` - Invalid plan format\n- `401 Unauthorized` - Invalid API key\n- `413 Payload Too Large` - Plan exceeds size limit\n\n---\n\n### Submit Plan Generation Form\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/plan-generation`\n\n**Description:** Generate a task plan from natural language description.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "description": "Create a blog post about AI and publish it",\n  "constraints": {\n    "max_duration_minutes": 60,\n    "required_approvals": ["content_review"]\n  },\n  "preferences": {\n    "style": "professional",\n    "tone": "informative"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "submission_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "generated",\n  "plan_id": "uuid",\n  "tasks": [\n    {\n      "id": "uuid",\n      "name": "Research topic",\n      "type": "research",\n      "estimated_duration_minutes": 15\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Submit Task Execution Form\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/forms/task-execution`\n\n**Description:** Execute a specific task.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "execution_mode": "automatic",\n  "parameters": {\n    "input_data": "...",\n    "options": {}\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "submission_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "executing",\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "execution_id": "uuid",\n  "estimated_completion": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Task Execution\n\n### Get Task Status\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/tasks/{task_id}/status`\n\n**Description:** Get current status of a task.\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "completed",\n  "progress": 100,\n  "result": {\n    "output": "...",\n    "metrics": {}\n  },\n  "started_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "completed_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Cancel Task\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/tasks/{task_id}/cancel`\n\n**Description:** Cancel a running task.\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "cancelled",\n  "cancelled_at": "2024-01-15T10:15:00Z"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Correction Capture\n\n### Submit Correction\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/corrections`\n\n**Description:** Submit a correction for a task execution.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "correction_type": "output_modification",\n  "original_value": "incorrect output",\n  "corrected_value": "correct output",\n  "reason": "The output had incorrect formatting",\n  "severity": "medium"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "correction_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "recorded",\n  "quality_score": 0.85,\n  "will_be_used_for_training": true\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Submit Feedback\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/feedback`\n\n**Description:** Submit feedback on task execution.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "feedback_type": "quality",\n  "rating": 4,\n  "comment": "Good result but could be faster",\n  "category": "performance"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "feedback_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "recorded",\n  "thank_you": true\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Get Corrections\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/corrections`\n\n**Query Parameters:**\n- `task_id` (optional) - Filter by task\n- `status` (optional) - Filter by status (pending, approved, rejected)\n- `limit` (optional) - Number of results (default: 50)\n- `offset` (optional) - Pagination offset\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "corrections": [\n    {\n      "id": "uuid",\n      "task_id": "uuid",\n      "type": "output_modification",\n      "status": "approved",\n      "created_at": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n    }\n  ],\n  "total": 100,\n  "limit": 50,\n  "offset": 0\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Shadow Agent\n\n### Make Prediction\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/shadow-agent/predict`\n\n**Description:** Get a prediction from the shadow agent.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "input_features": {\n    "task_type": "validation",\n    "complexity": 5,\n    "context": {}\n  },\n  "task_id": "uuid",\n  "use_fallback": true\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "prediction_id": "uuid",\n  "prediction": true,\n  "confidence": 0.92,\n  "source": "shadow_agent",\n  "model_version": "1.2.0",\n  "prediction_time_ms": 45\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Get Shadow Agent Stats\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/shadow-agent/stats`\n\n**Description:** Get statistics about shadow agent performance.\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "total_predictions": 10000,\n  "avg_confidence": 0.87,\n  "high_confidence_rate": 0.75,\n  "avg_prediction_time_ms": 52,\n  "fallback_rate": 0.15,\n  "current_model": {\n    "id": "uuid",\n    "version": "1.2.0",\n    "accuracy": 0.91\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Train Model\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/shadow-agent/train`\n\n**Description:** Trigger model training from recent corrections.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "model_name": "shadow_agent_v2",\n  "model_version": "2.0.0",\n  "tune_hyperparameters": true,\n  "min_corrections": 1000\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "training_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "started",\n  "estimated_duration_minutes": 30,\n  "model_id": "uuid"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Deploy Model\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/shadow-agent/deploy`\n\n**Description:** Deploy a trained model to production.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "model_id": "uuid",\n  "environment": "production",\n  "use_ab_test": true,\n  "use_gradual_rollout": true\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "deployment_id": "uuid",\n  "status": "deploying",\n  "model_id": "uuid",\n  "environment": "production",\n  "rollout_strategy": "gradual"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Health Check\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /health`\n\n**Description:** Check API health status.\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "status": "healthy",\n  "version": "1.0.0",\n  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z",\n  "components": {\n    "database": "healthy",\n    "redis": "healthy",\n    "shadow_agent": "healthy"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n### Get Metrics\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /metrics`\n\n**Description:** Get Prometheus metrics.\n\n**Response:** (Prometheus format)\n```\n# HELP murphy_api_requests_total Total API requests\n# TYPE murphy_api_requests_total counter\nmurphy_api_requests_total{method="GET",endpoint="/health"} 1000\n\n# HELP murphy_model_accuracy Current model accuracy\n# TYPE murphy_model_accuracy gauge\nmurphy_model_accuracy 0.91\n```\n\n---\n\n### Get System Status\n\n**Endpoint:** `GET /api/status`\n\n**Description:** Get complete system status.\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  "system": {\n    "status": "operational",\n    "uptime_seconds": 86400,\n    "version": "1.0.0"\n  },\n  "shadow_agent": {\n    "model_loaded": true,\n    "model_version": "1.2.0",\n    "accuracy": 0.91\n  },\n  "monitoring": {\n    "active_alerts": 0,\n    "last_check": "2024-01-15T10:00:00Z"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Error Responses\n\nAll error responses follow this format:\n\n```json\n{\n  "error": {\n    "code": "ERROR_CODE",\n    "message": "Human-readable error message",\n    "details": {\n      "field": "Additional context"\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### Common Error Codes\n\n- `INVALID_REQUEST` - Request validation failed\n- `UNAUTHORIZED` - Invalid or missing API key\n- `NOT_FOUND` - Resource not found\n- `RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` - Too many requests\n- `INTERNAL_ERROR` - Server error\n\n---\n\n## Rate Limiting\n\n- **Rate Limit:** 1000 requests per hour per API key\n- **Headers:**\n  - `X-RateLimit-Limit`: Maximum requests per hour\n  - `X-RateLimit-Remaining`: Remaining requests\n  - `X-RateLimit-Reset`: Time when limit resets (Unix timestamp)\n\n---\n\n## Webhooks\n\n### Configure Webhook\n\n**Endpoint:** `POST /api/webhooks`\n\n**Description:** Configure a webhook for events.\n\n**Request Body:**\n```json\n{\n  "url": "https://your-server.com/webhook",\n  "events": ["task.completed", "correction.submitted"],\n  "secret": "webhook-secret"\n}\n```\n\n### Webhook Events\n\n- `task.completed` - Task execution completed\n- `task.failed` - Task execution failed\n- `correction.submitted` - New correction submitted\n- `model.deployed` - New model deployed\n- `alert.triggered` - Alert triggered\n\n---\n\n## SDKs\n\n### Python SDK\n\n```python\nfrom murphy_client import MurphyClient\n\nclient = MurphyClient(api_key="your-api-key")\n\n# Submit task\nresult = client.tasks.execute(\n    task_id="uuid",\n    parameters={"input": "data"}\n)\n\n# Get prediction\nprediction = client.shadow_agent.predict(\n    input_features={"task_type": "validation"}\n)\n```\n\n### JavaScript SDK\n\n```javascript\nconst Murphy = require(\'murphy-client\');\n\nconst client = new Murphy({ apiKey: \'your-api-key\' });\n\n// Submit task\nconst result = await client.tasks.execute({\n  taskId: \'uuid\',\n  parameters: { input: \'data\' }\n});\n\n// Get prediction\nconst prediction = await client.shadowAgent.predict({\n  inputFeatures: { taskType: \'validation\' }\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n## Support\n\n- **Documentation:** https://docs.murphy-system.com\n- **API Status:** {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/deployment/USER_GUIDE.md">\n# Murphy System User Guide\n\n## Welcome to Murphy System\n\nMurphy System is an intelligent task execution platform that learns from your corrections and continuously improves its decision-making capabilities.\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n1. [Getting Started](#getting-started)\n2. [Core Concepts](#core-concepts)\n3. [Using the System](#using-the-system)\n4. [Training the Shadow Agent](#training-the-shadow-agent)\n5. [Best Practices](#best-practices)\n6. [Troubleshooting](#troubleshooting)\n\n---\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Prerequisites\n- API key (request from your administrator)\n- Python 3.11+ or Node.js 20+ (for SDK usage)\n- Basic understanding of task automation\n\n### Quick Start\n\n#### 1. Install the SDK\n\n**Python:**\n```bash\npip install murphy-client\n```\n\n**JavaScript:**\n```bash\nnpm install murphy-client\n```\n\n#### 2. Initialize the Client\n\n**Python:**\n```python\nfrom murphy_client import MurphyClient\n\nclient = MurphyClient(api_key="your-api-key")\n```\n\n**JavaScript:**\n```javascript\nconst Murphy = require(\'murphy-client\');\nconst client = new Murphy({ apiKey: \'your-api-key\' });\n```\n\n#### 3. Execute Your First Task\n\n**Python:**\n```python\n# Submit a task\nresult = client.tasks.execute(\n    description="Create a blog post about AI",\n    parameters={\n        "topic": "Artificial Intelligence",\n        "length": "medium",\n        "style": "professional"\n    }\n)\n\nprint(f"Task ID: {result.task_id}")\nprint(f"Status: {result.status}")\n```\n\n**JavaScript:**\n```javascript\n// Submit a task\nconst result = await client.tasks.execute({\n  description: "Create a blog post about AI",\n  parameters: {\n    topic: "Artificial Intelligence",\n    length: "medium",\n    style: "professional"\n  }\n});\n\nconsole.log(`Task ID: ${result.taskId}`);\nconsole.log(`Status: ${result.status}`);\n```\n\n---\n\n## Core Concepts\n\n### 1. Tasks\nTasks are units of work that Murphy executes. Each task has:\n- **Type:** The category of work (e.g., content creation, data processing)\n- **Parameters:** Input data and configuration\n- **Status:** Current state (pending, executing, completed, failed)\n- **Result:** Output data and metrics\n\n### 2. Plans\nPlans are collections of related tasks with dependencies:\n- **Sequential:** Tasks execute one after another\n- **Parallel:** Tasks execute simultaneously\n- **Conditional:** Tasks execute based on conditions\n\n### 3. Corrections\nWhen Murphy makes a mistake, you can submit corrections:\n- **Output Corrections:** Fix incorrect results\n- **Process Corrections:** Improve how tasks are executed\n- **Parameter Corrections:** Adjust input parameters\n\n### 4. Shadow Agent\nThe Shadow Agent learns from your corrections:\n- **Learns Patterns:** Identifies common correction patterns\n- **Improves Accuracy:** Gets better over time\n- **Provides Confidence:** Indicates certainty in decisions\n- **Falls Back:** Uses Murphy Gate when uncertain\n\n### 5. Murphy Gate\nThe deterministic validation system:\n- **Validates Tasks:** Checks if tasks should proceed\n- **Calculates Uncertainty:** Assesses risk levels\n- **Provides Fallback:** Used when Shadow Agent is uncertain\n\n---\n\n## Using the System\n\n### Creating and Executing Tasks\n\n#### Method 1: Natural Language Description\n\n```python\n# Describe what you want in plain English\nresult = client.tasks.create_from_description(\n    description="""\n    Research the latest trends in AI for 2024,\n    create a summary report, and email it to the team.\n    """\n)\n```\n\n#### Method 2: Structured Plan\n\n```python\n# Define a detailed plan\nplan = {\n    "name": "AI Research Report",\n    "tasks": [\n        {\n            "name": "Research AI trends",\n            "type": "research",\n            "parameters": {\n                "topic": "AI trends 2024",\n                "sources": ["academic", "industry"]\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            "name": "Create summary",\n            "type": "content_creation",\n            "depends_on": ["Research AI trends"],\n            "parameters": {\n                "format": "report",\n                "length": "2000 words"\n            }\n        },\n        {\n            "name": "Send email",\n            "type": "communication",\n            "depends_on": ["Create summary"],\n            "parameters": {\n                "recipients": ["team@company.com"],\n                "subject": "AI Trends Report 2024"\n            }\n        }\n    ]\n}\n\nresult = client.plans.submit(plan)\n```\n\n### Monitoring Task Progress\n\n```python\n# Get task status\nstatus = client.tasks.get_status(task_id)\n\nprint(f"Status: {status.status}")\nprint(f"Progress: {status.progress}%")\nprint(f"Estimated completion: {status.estimated_completion}")\n\n# Wait for completion\nresult = client.tasks.wait_for_completion(\n    task_id,\n    timeout_seconds=300,\n    poll_interval=5\n)\n```\n\n### Handling Task Results\n\n```python\n# Get task result\nresult = client.tasks.get_result(task_id)\n\nif result.status == "completed":\n    print("Task completed successfully!")\n    print(f"Output: {result.output}")\n    print(f"Metrics: {result.metrics}")\nelif result.status == "failed":\n    print(f"Task failed: {result.error}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## Submitting Corrections\n\n### When to Submit Corrections\n\nSubmit corrections when:\n- ✅ Output is incorrect or incomplete\n- ✅ Process could be improved\n- ✅ Parameters need adjustment\n- ✅ Task took too long\n- ✅ Resource usage was inefficient\n\n### How to Submit Corrections\n\n#### Output Correction\n\n```python\n# Correct an incorrect output\ncorrection = client.corrections.submit(\n    task_id=task_id,\n    correction_type="output_modification",\n    original_value="Incorrect output text",\n    corrected_value="Correct output text",\n    reason="The output had factual errors",\n    severity="high"\n)\n```\n\n#### Process Correction\n\n```python\n# Suggest process improvement\ncorrection = client.corrections.submit(\n    task_id=task_id,\n    correction_type="process_improvement",\n    suggestion="Use parallel processing for faster execution",\n    reason="Task took too long to complete",\n    severity="medium"\n)\n```\n\n#### Parameter Correction\n\n```python\n# Correct parameters\ncorrection = client.corrections.submit(\n    task_id=task_id,\n    correction_type="parameter_adjustment",\n    parameter_name="temperature",\n    original_value=0.9,\n    corrected_value=0.7,\n    reason="Output was too creative, needed more consistency",\n    severity="low"\n)\n```\n\n### Correction Best Practices\n\n1. **Be Specific:** Clearly explain what was wrong and why\n2. **Provide Context:** Include relevant information about the task\n3. **Rate Severity:** Help prioritize important corrections\n4. **Be Constructive:** Focus on improvement, not blame\n5. **Submit Promptly:** Correct issues as soon as you notice them\n\n---\n\n## Training the Shadow Agent\n\n### Understanding Training\n\nThe Shadow Agent learns from your corrections through:\n1. **Pattern Recognition:** Identifies common correction patterns\n2. **Feature Learning:** Understands what factors lead to errors\n3. **Confidence Calibration:** Learns when to be certain vs. uncertain\n4. **Continuous Improvement:** Gets better with more corrections\n\n### Monitoring Training Progress\n\n```python\n# Get training statistics\nstats = client.shadow_agent.get_stats()\n\nprint(f"Total corrections: {stats.total_corrections}")\nprint(f"Model accuracy: {stats.accuracy:.2%}")\nprint(f"Confidence: {stats.avg_confidence:.2%}")\nprint(f"Training data quality: {stats.data_quality_score:.2f}")\n```\n\n### Triggering Manual Training\n\n```python\n# Trigger training when you have enough corrections\ntraining = client.shadow_agent.train(\n    model_name="shadow_agent_v2",\n    tune_hyperparameters=True,\n    min_corrections=1000\n)\n\nprint(f"Training started: {training.training_id}")\nprint(f"Estimated duration: {training.estimated_duration_minutes} minutes")\n\n# Wait for training to complete\nresult = client.shadow_agent.wait_for_training(\n    training.training_id,\n    timeout_minutes=60\n)\n\nprint(f"Training completed!")\nprint(f"New model accuracy: {result.accuracy:.2%}")\n```\n\n### Deploying Trained Models\n\n```python\n# Deploy with gradual rollout\ndeployment = client.shadow_agent.deploy(\n    model_id=result.model_id,\n    environment="production",\n    use_gradual_rollout=True,\n    initial_traffic=0.1  # Start with 10% traffic\n)\n\nprint(f"Deployment started: {deployment.deployment_id}")\nprint(f"Initial traffic: {deployment.initial_traffic:.0%}")\n```\n\n---\n\n## Best Practices\n\n### 1. Task Design\n\n**DO:**\n- ✅ Break complex tasks into smaller subtasks\n- ✅ Provide clear, specific descriptions\n- ✅ Include relevant context and constraints\n- ✅ Set realistic timeouts and resource limits\n\n**DON\'T:**\n- ❌ Create overly complex single tasks\n- ❌ Use vague or ambiguous descriptions\n- ❌ Omit important context\n- ❌ Set unrealistic expectations\n\n### 2. Correction Submission\n\n**DO:**\n- ✅ Submit corrections promptly\n- ✅ Provide detailed explanations\n- ✅ Include examples when helpful\n- ✅ Rate severity appropriately\n\n**DON\'T:**\n- ❌ Delay correction submission\n- ❌ Submit vague corrections\n- ❌ Over-correct minor issues\n- ❌ Submit duplicate corrections\n\n### 3. Model Training\n\n**DO:**\n- ✅ Wait for sufficient corrections (1000+)\n- ✅ Validate data quality before training\n- ✅ Use gradual rollout for new models\n- ✅ Monitor performance after deployment\n\n**DON\'T:**\n- ❌ Train with insufficient data\n- ❌ Deploy without testing\n- ❌ Rush to 100% traffic\n- ❌ Ignore performance metrics\n\n### 4. Monitoring\n\n**DO:**\n- ✅ Check system status regularly\n- ✅ Review performance metrics\n- ✅ Respond to alerts promptly\n- ✅ Track improvement over time\n\n**DON\'T:**\n- ❌ Ignore alerts\n- ❌ Skip regular reviews\n- ❌ Neglect performance trends\n- ❌ Overlook quality issues\n\n---\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n#### Issue: Task Stuck in "Executing" State\n\n**Solution:**\n```python\n# Check task status\nstatus = client.tasks.get_status(task_id)\n\n# If stuck for too long, cancel and retry\nif status.duration_minutes > 60:\n    client.tasks.cancel(task_id)\n    # Resubmit with adjusted parameters\n```\n\n#### Issue: Low Shadow Agent Confidence\n\n**Solution:**\n- Submit more corrections for similar tasks\n- Check if task type is well-represented in training data\n- Consider using Murphy Gate fallback\n\n#### Issue: Incorrect Results\n\n**Solution:**\n1. Submit a correction immediately\n2. Review task parameters\n3. Check if similar tasks have corrections\n4. Consider retraining the model\n\n#### Issue: Slow Performance\n\n**Solution:**\n- Check system status\n- Review resource usage\n- Consider breaking task into smaller parts\n- Contact support if persistent\n\n---\n\n## Getting Help\n\n### Resources\n- **Documentation:** https://docs.murphy-system.com\n- **API Reference:** https://api.murphy-system.com/docs\n- **Community Forum:** https://community.murphy-system.com\n- **Video Tutorials:** https://tutorials.murphy-system.com\n\n### Support Channels\n- **Email:** support@murphy-system.com\n- **Chat:** Available in dashboard\n- **Phone:** +1-XXX-XXX-XXXX (Business hours)\n\n### Feedback\nWe value your feedback! Clone Repository\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/your-org/murphy-system.git\ncd murphy-system\n```\n\n### 2. Install Dependencies\n\n```bash\n# Create virtual environment\npython -m venv venv\nsource venv/bin/activate  # On Windows: venv\\Scripts\\activate\n\n# Install dependencies\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n### 3. Configure Environment\n\n```bash\n# Copy example environment file\ncp .env.example .env\n\n# Edit configuration\nnano .env\n```\n\n**Required Environment Variables:**\n```bash\nMURPHY_ENV=development\nMURPHY_DATA_DIR=/app/data\nMURPHY_LOG_DIR=/app/logs\nDATABASE_URL=postgresql://murphy:murphy@localhost:5432/murphy\nREDIS_URL=redis://localhost:6379/0\nAPI_KEY=your-development-api-key\n```\n\n### 4. {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="murphy_implementation/deployment/load-test.js">\n/**\n * Murphy System Load Test\n * \n * This script performs load testing on the Murphy System API\n * using k6 (https://k6.io/)\n * \n * Usage: k6 run load-test.js\n */\n\nimport http from \'k6/http\';\nimport { check, sleep } from \'k6\';\nimport { Rate, Trend } from \'k6/metrics\';\n\n// Custom metrics\nconst errorRate = new Rate(\'errors\');\nconst apiResponseTime = new Trend(\'api_response_time\');\n\n// Test configuration\nexport const options = {\n  stages: [\n    { duration: \'2m\', target: 50 },   // Ramp up to 50 users\n    { duration: \'5m\', target: 50 },   // Stay at 50 users\n    { duration: \'2m\', target: 100 },  // Ramp up to 100 users\n    { duration: \'5m\', target: 100 },  // Stay at 100 users\n    { duration: \'2m\', target: 200 },  // Ramp up to 200 users\n    { duration: \'5m\', target: 200 },  // Stay at 200 users\n    { duration: \'5m\', target: 0 },    // Ramp down to 0 users\n  ],\n  thresholds: {\n    \'http_req_duration\': [\'p(95)<1000\'], // 95% of requests should be below 1s\n    \'errors\': [\'rate<0.1\'],              // Error rate should be below 10%\n    \'http_req_failed\': [\'rate<0.05\'],    // Failed requests should be below 5%\n  },\n};\n\n// Configuration\nconst BASE_URL = __ENV.BASE_URL || \'http://localhost:8000\';\nconst API_KEY = __ENV.API_KEY || \'test-api-key\';\n\nconst headers = {\n  \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n  \'X-API-Key\': API_KEY,\n};\n\n// Test scenarios\nexport default function () {\n  // Scenario 1: Health Check (10% of requests)\n  if (Math.random() < 0.1) {\n    testHealthCheck();\n  }\n  \n  // Scenario 2: Task Submission (40% of requests)\n  else if (Math.random() < 0.5) {\n    testTaskSubmission();\n  }\n  \n  // Scenario 3: Task Status Check (30% of requests)\n  else if (Math.random() < 0.8) {\n    testTaskStatus();\n  }\n  \n  // Scenario 4: Shadow Agent Prediction (20% of requests)\n  else {\n    testShadowAgentPrediction();\n  }\n  \n  sleep(1);\n}\n\nfunction testHealthCheck() {\n  const res = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/health`);\n  \n  const success = check(res, {\n    \'health check status is 200\': (r) => r.status === 200,\n    \'health check response time < 200ms\': (r) => r.timings.duration < 200,\n  });\n  \n  errorRate.add(!success);\n  apiResponseTime.add(res.timings.duration);\n}\n\nfunction testTaskSubmission() {\n  const payload = JSON.stringify({\n    description: \'Test task for load testing\',\n    parameters: {\n      test: true,\n      timestamp: Date.now(),\n    },\n  });\n  \n  const res = http.post(\n    `${BASE_URL}/api/forms/task-execution`,\n    payload,\n    { headers }\n  );\n  \n  const success = check(res, {\n    \'task submission status is 200\': (r) => r.status === 200,\n    \'task submission has task_id\': (r) => {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n        return body.task_id !== undefined;\n      } catch (e) {\n        return false;\n      }\n    },\n    \'task submission response time < 1000ms\': (r) => r.timings.duration < 1000,\n  });\n  \n  errorRate.add(!success);\n  apiResponseTime.add(res.timings.duration);\n}\n\nfunction testTaskStatus() {\n  // Use a mock task ID for testing\n  const taskId = \'test-task-\' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000);\n  \n  const res = http.get(\n    `${BASE_URL}/api/tasks/${taskId}/status`,\n    { headers }\n  );\n  \n  const success = check(res, {\n    \'task status response received\': (r) => r.status === 200 || r.status === 404,\n    \'task status response time < 500ms\': (r) => r.timings.duration < 500,\n  });\n  \n  errorRate.add(!success);\n  apiResponseTime.add(res.timings.duration);\n}\n\nfunction testShadowAgentPrediction() {\n  const payload = JSON.stringify({\n    input_features: {\n      task_type: \'validation\',\n      complexity: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10),\n      context: {\n        test: true,\n      },\n    },\n    use_fallback: true,\n  });\n  \n  const res = http.post(\n    `${BASE_URL}/api/shadow-agent/predict`,\n    payload,\n    { headers }\n  );\n  \n  const success = check(res, {\n    \'prediction status is 200\': (r) => r.status === 200,\n    \'prediction has confidence\': (r) => {\n      try {\n        const body = JSON.parse(r.body);\n        return body.confidence !== undefined;\n      } catch (e) {\n        return false;\n      }\n    },\n    \'prediction response time < 500ms\': (r) => r.timings.duration < 500,\n  });\n  \n  errorRate.add(!success);\n  apiResponseTime.add(res.timings.duration);\n}\n\n// Setup function (runs once at the start)\nexport function setup() {\n  console.log(\'Starting load test...\');\n  console.log(`Base URL: ${BASE_URL}`);\n  console.log(`API Key: ${API_KEY.substring(0, 10)}...`);\n  \n  // Verify API is accessible\n  const res = http.get(`${BASE_URL}/health`);\n  if (res.status !== 200) {\n    throw new Error(`API not accessible: ${res.status}`);\n  }\n  \n  console.log(\'API is accessible, starting test...\');\n}\n\n// Teardown function (runs once at the end)\nexport function teardown(data) {\n  console.log(\'Load test completed!\');\n}\n\n// Handle summary\nexport function handleSummary(data) {\n  return {\n    \'load-test-results.json\': JSON.stringify(data, null, 2),\n    stdout: textSummary(data, { indent: \' \', enableColors: true }),\n  };\n}\n\nfunction textSummary(data, options) {\n  const indent = options.indent || \'\';\n  const enableColors = options.enableColors || false;\n  \n  let summary = \'\\n\';\n  summary += `${indent}Load Test Summary\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}================\\n\\n`;\n  \n  // Requests\n  summary += `${indent}Requests:\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Total: ${data.metrics.http_reqs.values.count}\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Rate: ${data.metrics.http_reqs.values.rate.toFixed(2)}/s\\n\\n`;\n  \n  // Response times\n  summary += `${indent}Response Times:\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Avg: ${data.metrics.http_req_duration.values.avg.toFixed(2)}ms\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Min: ${data.metrics.http_req_duration.values.min.toFixed(2)}ms\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Max: ${data.metrics.http_req_duration.values.max.toFixed(2)}ms\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  p(95): ${data.metrics.http_req_duration.values[\'p(95)\'].toFixed(2)}ms\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  p(99): ${data.metrics.http_req_duration.values[\'p(99)\'].toFixed(2)}ms\\n\\n`;\n  \n  // Errors\n  summary += `${indent}Errors:\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Rate: ${(data.metrics.errors.values.rate * 100).toFixed(2)}%\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Failed Requests: ${(data.metrics.http_req_failed.values.rate * 100).toFixed(2)}%\\n\\n`;\n  \n  // Virtual Users\n  summary += `${indent}Virtual Users:\\n`;\n  summary += `${indent}  Max: ${data.metrics.vus_max.values.max}\\n\\n`;\n  \n  // Thresholds\n  summary += `${indent}Thresholds:\\n`;\n  for (const [name, threshold] of Object.entries(data.thresholds)) {\n    const passed = threshold.ok ? \'✓\' : \'✗\';\n    summary += `${indent}  ${passed} ${name}\\n`;\n  }\n  \n  return summary;\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}
